; classification option (inside `building` and before first `levels`)
; Example:
;	 classification core|defence|military|trade|water|culture|religious (deprecated, but recognised:fortification|infrastructure|other)
; This tells the game which category of the building browser to use.
; RomeHD has subtly different classifications than the original, so note the deprecated classifications, they wont work anymore.
; If no classification is specified, the game will guess based on the building name, which works for all the unmodded buildings.
; Automatic classification:
;   core_building
;	   core
;   defenses
;	   defence
;   barracks|equestrian|missiles|smith|despotic_law
;	   military
;   market|port_buildings|hinterland_*|caravans
;	   trade
;   health
;	   water
;   academic|amphitheatres|theatres|taverns
;	   culture
;   temple_*|christian_acedemic
;	   religious
; Explicit classification overrides the automatic classification, so if you don't like the above classifications, you can overule them.

;;exclusivity tags, used for the "no_building_tagged" condition
tags
{
	temple
	roman_gov
	greek_gov
	generic_gov
}

;;alises, give multiple conditions a string (or allow conditions with normally no string to display one)
; alias roman_marian_reforms_triggered
; {
; 	requires factions { roman, } and major_event "marian_reforms"
;
; 	display_string roman_marian_reforms ;;gets a string from expanded_bi
; 	;; if display_string isn't included it will just display the strings for the events normally
; }

alias no_other_temple
{
	requires no_building_tagged temple queued

	display_string SMT_TECH_TREE_THREAD_REQUIRES_TEMPLE_DESTRUCTION
}

alias pre_camillan
{
	requires not major_event "camillan_reforms" and not major_event "manipular_reforms" and not major_event "polybian_reforms" and not major_event "marian_reforms"
}

alias camillan
{
	requires major_event "camillan_reforms" and not major_event "polybian_reforms" and not major_event "marian_reforms" 
}

alias pre_manipular
{
	requires major_event "camillan_reforms" and not major_event "manipular_reforms" and not major_event "polybian_reforms" and not major_event "marian_reforms" 
}

alias manipular
{
	requires major_event "manipular_reforms" and not major_event "polybian_reforms" and not major_event "marian_reforms" 
}

alias polybian
{
	requires major_event "polybian_reforms" and not major_event "marian_reforms"
}

alias marian
{
	requires major_event "marian_reforms" or major_event "marian_reforms_rise"
}

alias alexander
{
	requires factions { macedon, } and not major_event "antigonid_reforms"
}

alias antigonid
{
	requires major_event "antigonid_reforms"

;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;
;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;Roman government ;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;
;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;

alias roman_has_direct
{
	requires roman_faction and building_present hinterland_roman_praefectura or building_present hinterland_roman_municipium or building_present hinterland_roman_colonia_latina or building_present hinterland_roman_colonia
}

alias roman_has_allied
{
	requires roman_faction and building_present hinterland_roman_civitas
}

alias roman_has_gov
{
	requires roman_has_direct or roman_has_allied
}

alias roman_has_foedus
{
	requires roman_faction and building_present_min_level hinterland_roman_civitas roman_civitas_foederata
}

alias roman_has_rights
{
	requires building_present hinterland_roman_municipium or building_present hinterland_roman_colonia_latina or building_present hinterland_roman_colonia
}

alias no_other_roman_government
{
	requires no_building_tagged roman_gov queued
}

alias no_civitas
{
	requires not building_present_min_level hinterland_roman_civitas roman_civitas
}

alias no_colonia
{
	requires not building_present hinterland_roman_colonia
}

alias no_colonia_both
{
	requires not building_present hinterland_roman_colonia_latina and not building_present hinterland_roman_colonia
}

alias no_municipium
{
	requires not building_present hinterland_roman_municipium
}

alias no_praefectura
{
	requires not building_present hinterland_roman_praefectura
}

alias yes_civitas
{
	requires building_present_min_level hinterland_roman_civitas roman_civitas
}

alias yes_municipium
{
	requires building_present_min_level hinterland_roman_municipium roman_municipium_2
}

alias roman_faction_has_gov
{
	requires roman_faction and roman_has_gov
}

	requires building_present hinterland_greek_katoikia

{
	requires building_present hinterland_greek_klerouchia
}

	requires building_present hinterland_greek_polis

{
	requires greek_faction and greek_phrourion and location_greek
}

	requires greek_faction and greek_katoikia

	requires greek_phrourion or greek_katoikia or greek_klerouchia or greek_polis
}

{
	requires not greek_has_gov
}

;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;
;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;Generic governments ;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;
;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;

alias military_occupation_present
{
	requires building_present_min_level hinterland_gov_military_1 military_occupation
}

alias military_administration_present
{
	requires building_present_min_level hinterland_gov_military_2 military_administration
}

alias military_either_present
{
	requires military_occupation_present or military_administration_present
}

alias early_colony_present
{
	requires building_present_min_level hinterland_gov_colony_1 early_colony
}

alias full_colony_present
{
	requires building_present_min_level hinterland_gov_colony_2 full_colony
}

alias integrated_state_present
{
	requires building_present_min_level hinterland_gov_direct_1 integrated_state
}

alias free_state_present
{
	requires building_present_min_level hinterland_gov_allied_1 free_state
}

alias allied_state_present
{
	requires building_present_min_level hinterland_gov_allied_2 allied_state
}

alias tributary_state_present
{
	requires building_present_min_level hinterland_gov_allied_3 tributary_state
}

alias free_or_allied_present
{
	requires free_state_present or allied_state_present
}

alias military_or_early_colony_present
{
	requires military_either_present or early_colony_present
}

alias any_non_direct_present
{
	requires military_either_present or early_colony_present or full_colony_present or free_or_allied_present or tributary_state_present
}

alias no_other_government
{
	requires no_building_tagged generic_gov queued
}

;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;HIDDEN RESOURCE ALIASES ;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;;

}

alias blockaded_or_besieged
{
	requires hidden_resource blockaded or hidden_resource besieged
}

	requires resource marble or resource stone

{
	requires resource purple_dye or resource incense or resource silk

{

alias tradable_low
{
	requires resource pottery or resource hides or resource salt

alias tradable_resources
{
	requires tradable_high or tradable_medium or tradable_low
}
